No. 2,252 – fRiDAy,   OCtOBER  29, 2021
ImPORTANT   NOTICE   REGARDING   ACCEPTANCE   Of  NOTICES  
fOR  PubLICATION   IN  ThE  WEEkLy  “GAzETTE ”
AttENtiON  is drawn to the Notification appearing in the 1st week of every month, regarding the latest dates and times of acceptance of Notices 
for publication in the weekly Gazettes, at the end of every weekly Gazette of Democratic Socialist Republic of Sri Lanka.
All notices to be published in the weekly Gazettes shall close at 12.00 noon of each friday, two weeks before the date of publication. 
All Government Departments, Corporations, Boards, etc. are hereby advised that Notifications fixing closing dates and times of applications in 
respect of Post-Vacancies, Examinations, tender Notices and dates and times of Auction Sales, etc. should be prepared by giving adequate time 
both from the date of despatch of notices to Govt. Press and from the date of publication, thereby enabling those interested in the contents of such 
notices to actively and positively participate please note that inquiries and complaints made in respect of corrections pertaining to notification will 
not be entertained after three months from the date of publication.
All Notices to be published in the weekly Gazette should reach Government Press two weeks before the date of publication i.e. Notices 
for publication in the weekly Gazette of 19th November, 2021 should reach Government Press on or before 12.00 noon on 05th November, 2021.
Electronic Transactions Act, No. 19 of  2006 - Section 9
“Where any Act or enactment provides that any proclamation, rule, regulation, order, by-law, notification or other matter shall be 
published in the Gazette, then such requirement shall be deemed to have been satisfied if such rule, regulation, order, by-law, notification or other 
matter is published in an electronic form of the Gazette.”
 Gangani Liyanage,
 Government Printer.
Department of Govt. Printing, 
Colombo 08,
01st January, 2021.
  This Gazette can be downloaded from www.documents.gov.lk

At a meeting held on 30th August 2019 the Board of 
Directors of Commercial Bank of Ceylon PLC resolved 
specially and unanimously as follows:-
Whereas francis Hewakuruppu carrying on business 
as the Sole Proprietor under the name and style of 
“Neptune tea factory” as the obligor has made default in 
the payment due on Bond Nos. 6687 dated 30th December 
2003 attested by B. L. Wickramarachchi, Notary Public 
of Colombo, 369 dated 28th June 2004 attested by J. M. P. 
S. Jayaweera, Notary Public of Colombo, 132 dated 18th 
September 2014 and 159 dated 23rd January 2015 both 
attested by P. A. D. C. K. Perera, Notary Public of Galle 
and 070 dated 20th October 2015 attested by P. S. L. De 
Silva, Notary Public of Galle in favour of Commercial 
Bank of Ceylon Limited now known as Commercial 
Bank of Ceylon PLC (the land together with the tea 
factory and machinery morefully described in the 1st 
and 2nd Schedules hereto) and on Bond Nos. 3535 dated

attested by J. R. Gamage, Notary Public of Colombo, 36 
dated 5th April 2013 attested by P. A. D. C. K. Perera, 
Notary Public of Galle, in favour of Commercial Bank 
of Ceylon PLC formerly known as Commercial Bank of 
Ceylon Limited (the land inclusive of the tea factory 
morefully described in the 1st Schedule hereto)
And whereas francis Hewakuruppu carrying on business 
as  the Sole Proprietor under the name and style of “Neptune 
tea factory” as the obligor has made default in the payment 
due on Bond Nos. 4187 dated 15th September 2010 attested 
by J. R. Gamage, Notary Public of Colombo in favour of 
Commercial Bank of Ceylon PLC (the land morefully 
described in the 3rd Schedule hereto) and on Bond Nos. 
071 dated 20th October 2015 attested by P. S. L. De Silva, 
Notary Public of Galle and 16069 dated 24th August 2016 
attested by P. G. C. Nanayakkara, Notary Public of Matara 
in favour of Commercial Bank of Ceylon PLC (the land 
inclusive of the tea factory morefully described in the 3rd 
Schedule hereto and machinery morefully described in the 
4th Schedule hereto).
And whereas there is now due and owing to the 
Commercial Bank of Ceylon PLC as at 5th July 2019 a 
sum of Rupees One Hundred and Seventeen Million forty-
seven thousand Nine Hundred and Seventy-five and Cents 
twenty-one (Rs. 117,047,975.21) on the said Bonds and 
the Board of Directors of Commercial Bank of Ceylon PLC 
under the powers vested by Recovery of Loans by Banks 
(Special Provisions) Act No. 4 of 1990 do hereby resolve that 
the properties and premises inclusive of the tea factories 
and machineries morefully described in the 1st, 2nd and 3rd 
Schedules hereto and mortgaged to the Commercial Bank 
of Ceylon PLC formerly known as Commercial Bank of 
Ceylon Limited by the said Bond Nos. 6687, 369, 132, 159, 
070, 3535, 3781, 36, 4187, 071 and 16069 be sold by Public 
Auctions by Mr. L. B. Senanayake, Licensed Auctioneer 
of No. 200, 2nd floor, Hulftsdorp Street, Colombo 12 for 
the recovery of the said sum of Rupees One Hundred and 
Seventeen Million forty-seven thousand Nine Hundred 
and Seventy-five and Cents twenty-one (Rs. 117,047, 
975.21) with further interest on a sum of Rs. 54,899,835.60 
at 10.50% per annum and on a sum of Rs. 12,566,677/- at 
PLR+2.00% per annum (Present Rate - 14.09% per annum)  
and on a sum of Rs. 37,521,119.32 at PLR + 3.00% per 
annum (Present Rate - 15.09% per annum) from 6th July 
2019 to date of sale together with costs of advertising and 
any other charges incurred less payments (if any) since 
received.
